  CODE
  {
    VAR
      PrintContactRealization@1100525009 : Boolean;
      PrintGeneral@1100525008 : Boolean;
      PrintDescription@1100525007 : Boolean;
      PrintExplanation@1100525006 : Boolean;
      PrintElements@1100525005 : Boolean;
      PrintConditions@1100525004 : Boolean;
      PrintUserDefinedTexts@1100525003 : Boolean;
      PrintBidForm@1100525002 : Boolean;
      PrintCoverPage@1100525001 : Boolean;
      PrintPageHeaders@1100525000 : Boolean;
      TextExpr@1100525010 : Text[250];

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF "Construction Specification RAW".GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', "Construction Specification RAW".TABLECAPTION, "Construction Specification RAW".GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE BuildParagraphNo@1100525002(ChapterNo@1100525000 : Code[2];ParagraphNo@1100525001 : Code[2];SectionNo@1100525002 : Code[2];SubsectionNo@1100525003 : Code[2]) Result : Code[20];
    BEGIN
      Result := ChapterNo;

      IF ParagraphNo = '00' THEN
        EXIT;

      Result := STRSUBSTNO('%1.%2', Result, ParagraphNo);

      IF SectionNo = '00' THEN
        EXIT;

      Result := STRSUBSTNO('%1.%2', Result, SectionNo);

      IF SubsectionNo = '00' THEN
        EXIT;

      Result := STRSUBSTNO('%1.%2', Result, SubsectionNo);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value = 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Shared offset As Integer
Shared newgroup As Object
Shared currentgroup1 As Object
Shared currentgroup2 As Object

Public Function GetGroupPageNumber(newgroup2 As Boolean, pagenumber As Integer) As Object
    If newgroup2
        offset = pagenumber - 1
    End If
    Return pagenumber - offset
End Function

Public Function InNewGroup(group1 As Object, group2 As Object) As Boolean
    newgroup = False
    If Not (group1 = currentgroup1)
        newgroup = True
        currentgroup2 = group2
        currentgroup1 = group1
    Else
        If Not (group2 = currentgroup2)
            newgroup = True
            currentgroup2 = group2
        End If
    End If
    Return newgroup
End Function

Shared Data1 As Object

Public Function GetData(Num As Integer) As Object
    Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1), Chr(177))))
End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData As Object)
    If NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
        Data1 = NewData
    End If
End Function


Shared Data2 As Decimal

Public Function GetData2() As Decimal
    Return Data2
End Function

Public Function SetData2(Reset As Boolean, NewData As Decimal) As Boolean
    If (NewData &lt;&gt; 0) Or Reset Then
        Data2 = NewData
    End If
    Return True
End Function


Shared LinesPrinted As Boolean

Public Function SetLinesPrinted(NewData As Boolean) As Boolean
    LinesPrinted = NewData
    Return True
End Function

Public Function GetLinesPrinted() As Boolean
    Return LinesPrinted
End Function
